PART I : SEC. (I) - GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY  OF THE DEMOCRATIC  SOCIALIST  REPUBLIC  OF  SRI  LANKA - 02.11.2017
1A
(CHAPTER 252)  MUNICIPAL  COUNCILS  ORDINANCE
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under sections 2, 5 and 10 of the Municipal Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) to be
read with Section 18 of the Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I, Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of Provincial Councils
and Local Government, do by this order, further amend the order published in the Gazette Extraordinary  No. 329/8 of
10th August, 1978 relating to the Colombo Municipal Council  as follows:
1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;
“(4) Determine that the  Colombo Municipal Council  shall consist of such number of members to be elected and
returned in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Sixty Six members to be elected under paragraph (a) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the Municipal Councils
Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
ii. Forty Four members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the
Municipal Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
iii. Such number of members determined by the Commissioner of Elections under paragraph (a) subsection (4)
of Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of paragraph (c) of Sub-
section (1) of Section 5 of the Municipal Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252)”
2. The term of office of the members of this Municipal Council shall commence with effect from 15th February, 2018.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
01st November, 2017.

PART I : SEC. (I) - GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY  OF  THE DEMOCRATIC   SOCIALIST   REPUBLIC OF  SRI  LANKA - 02.11.2017
2A
(CHAPTER 252)  MUNICIPAL  COUNCILS  ORDINANCE
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under sections 2, 5 and 10 of the  Municipal Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) to be
read with Section 18 of the Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I, Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of Provincial Councils
and Local Government, do by this order, further amend the order published in the Gazette Extraordinary  No. 329/8 of
10th August, 1978 relating to the Dehiwala-Mt. Lavinia Municipal Council  as follows:
1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;
“(4) Determine that the Dehiwala-Mt. Lavinia Municipal Council  shall consist of such number of members to be
elected and returned in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Twenty Nine members to be elected under paragraph (a) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the Municipal
Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
ii. Nineteen  members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the
Municipal Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
iii. Such number of members determined by the Commissioner of Elections under paragraph (a) subsection (4)
of Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of paragraph (c) of Sub-
section (1) of Section 5 of the Municipal Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252)”
2. The term of office of the members of this Municipal Council shall commence with effect from 15th February, 2018.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
01st November, 2017.

elected and returned in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Twenty One members to be elected under paragraph (a) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the Municipal Councils
Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;
ii. Fourteen members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of subsection (1) of section 5 of the Municipal
Councils Ordinance (Chapter 252) ;

Order

read with Section 18 of the Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I, Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of Provincial Councils

1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;

in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Eleven members to be elected under paragraph (a) of Sub-section (1) of section 5 of the Urban Councils
Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;
ii. Seven members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban
Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;
iii. Such number of members determined by the Commissioner of Elections under paragraph (a) Sub-section (4)
of Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of paragraph (c) of Sub-
section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255)”
2. The term of office of the members of this Urban Council shall commence with effect from 15th February, 2018.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
01st November, 2017.

(CHAPTER 255)  URBAN  COUNCILS  ORDINANCE
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under sections 2, 5 and 10 of Urban Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) to be read with
Section 18 of the Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2)  I, Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of Provincial Councils and Local
Government, do by this order, further amend the order which was finally amended by the Gazette Extraordinary
No. 453/4 of 12th May, 1987, published in the Gazette Extraordinary  No. 329/8 of 10th August, 1978 relating to the
Seethawakapura Urban Council  as follows:
1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;
“(4) Determine that the Seethawakapura Urban Council shall consist of such number of members to be elected and
returned in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Fourteen members to be elected under paragraph (a) of Sub-section (1) of section 5 of the Urban Councils
Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;
ii. Nine members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban
Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;
iii. Such number of members determined by the Commissioner of Elections under paragraph (a) of Sub-section
(4) of Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of paragraph (c) of
Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban  Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255)”
2. The term of office of the members of this Urban Council shall commence with effect from 15th February, 2018.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
01st November, 2017.

PRADESHIYA  SABHAS  ACT,  No.  15  OF  1987
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Sub-section (1) of  Section 2, Section 4 and Section 6 of the Pradeshiya
Sabhas Act,  No. 15 of 1987 to be read with Section 18 of Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I, Faiszer Musthapha,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government, do by this order, further amend the order, published in the Gazette
Extraordinary No. 453/5 of 12th May, 1987 relating to the Seethawaka Pradeshiya Sabha  as follows:
1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;
“(4) Determine that the  Seethawaka Pradeshiya Sabha  shall consist of such number of members to be elected
and returned in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Twenty Six members to be elected under paragraph (a) of Sub-section (1) of section 4 of the Pradeshiya Sabhas
Act, No. 15 of 1987;
ii. Seventeen members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of Sub-section (1) of Section 4 of the
Pradeshiya Sabhas Act, No. 15 of 1987;

<!-- page 8 -->

of Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of paragraph (b) of Sub-

2. The term of office of the members of this Pradeshiya Sabha shall commence with effect from 15th February, 2018.

PRADESHIYA  SABHAS  ACT,  No.  15  OF  1987
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under Sub-section (1) of  Section 2, Section 4 and Section 6 of the Pradeshiya Sabhas
Act , No. 15 of 1987 to be read with Section 18 of Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I, Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of
Provincial Councils and Local Government, do by this order, further amend the order, published in the Gazette Extraordinary
No. 453/5 of 12th May, 1987 relating to the Homagama Pradeshiya Sabha as follows:
1. By the substitution for paragraph (4) thereof, of the following paragraph ;
“(4) Determine that the Homagama Pradeshiya Sabha  shall consist of such number of members to be elected and
returned in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Twenty-Eight members to be elected under paragraph (a) of Sub-section (1) of Section 4 of the Pradeshiya
Sabhas Act, No. 15 of 1987;
ii. Eighteen members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of Sub-section (1) of Section 4 of the
Pradeshiya Sabhas Act, No. 15 of 1987;
iii. Such number of members determined by the Commissioner of Elections under paragraph (a) of Sub-section
(4) of Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of paragraph (b) of
Sub-section (1) of Section 4 of the Pradeshiya Sabhas Act,, No. 15 of 1987”
2. The term of office of the members of this Pradeshiya Sabha shall commence with effect from 15th February, 2018.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
01st November, 2017.

(CHAPTER 255)  URBAN  COUNCILS  ORDINANCE
Order
BY virtue of the powers vested in me under sections 2, 5 and 10 of Urban Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) to be read with
Section 18 of the Interpretation Ordinance (Chapter 2), I, Faiszer Musthapha, Minister of Provincial Councils and Local
Government, do by this order, further amend the order published in the Gazette Extraordinary No. 231/13 of  09th February,
1983 relating to the Wattala-Mabola Urban Council as follows:
1. By the  amendment of the number of members mentioned in the Schedule thereof, follows :
“(4) Determine that the Wattala-Mabola Urban Council shall consist of such number of members to be elected and
returned in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.
i. Ten  members to be elected under paragraph (a) of Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban Councils
Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;
ii. Six members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban
Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;
iii. Such number of members determined by the Commissioner of Elections under paragraph (a) Sub-section (4)
of Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of paragraph (c) of Sub-
section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255)”
     2. The term of office of the members of this Urban Council shall commence with effect from 15th February, 2018.
F
AISZER MUSTHAPHA,
Minister of Provincial Councils and Local Government.
Colombo,
01st November, 2017.

Sabhas  Act, No. 15 of 1987;

(4) of Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of paragraph (b) of

returned in terms of following i, ii and iii sub paragraphs.

Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;

Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;

section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255)”
   2. The term of office of the members of this Urban Council shall commence with effect from 15th February, 2018.

Order

and returned in terms of following i, ii and iii Sub paragraphs.

Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;
ii. Nine members to be elected and returned under paragraph (b) of Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the
Urban Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255) ;

Sub-section (4) of  Section 65B of the Local Authorities Elections Ordinance (Chapter 262) in terms of
paragraph (c) of Sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the Urban Councils Ordinance (Chapter 255)”
2. The term of office of the members of this Urban Council shall commence with effect from 15th  February, 2018.
